margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. &#9744;</p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:4.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #7f7f7f">&#160;</p></div></div> <p style="page-break-before:always"></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"> <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&#160;30, 2022, Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter ended May&#160;31, 2022 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">7.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Regulation FD Disclosure</span>.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&#160;30, 2022, the Company is conducting a conference call and webcast beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time regarding its results for the fiscal quarter ended May&#160;31, 2022 and related matters.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Slides prepared for the purposes of the conference call are available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2022 Third Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">Strong Execution Across Segments; Results Broadly In Line with Expectations </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Third quarter highlights </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><I></I>Third quarter earnings per share (EPS*) from continuing operations decreased 73.8&nbsp;percent to $0.33, compared
with EPS of $1.27 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; continuing operations adjusted** EPS decreased 30.0&nbsp;percent to $0.96, down 28.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis against strong growth of
93.6&nbsp;percent in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting peak <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccine volumes </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-date</FONT></FONT> EPS from continuing operations
increased 190.6&nbsp;percent to $5.49, compared with EPS of $1.89 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; continuing operations adjusted EPS increased 13.3&nbsp;percent to $4.23, up 13.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency
basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $32.6&nbsp;billion, down 2.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis including a 720 basis point impact from AllianceRx Walgreens as anticipated </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

income of $1.1&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; adjusted operating income from continuing operations was $1.0&nbsp;billion, down 33.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill., June&nbsp;30, 2022&#151;Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2022, which
ended May&nbsp;31, 2022. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Chief Executive Officer Rosalind Brewer said: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;WBA delivered strong execution across operating segments and against very robust growth last year. Third quarter results were broadly in line with our
expectations, demonstrating the resilience of our business through our deep community connections and relevance to consumers. Walgreens Health achieved 65&nbsp;percent pro forma sales growth with progress on several fronts, including adding Buckeye
Health Plan as a strategic partner, already exceeding our 2022 target for covered lives, and launching our clinical trials business. With our decision to conclude the Boots strategic review, I firmly believe that our strategic actions are working to
deliver long-term shareholder value.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Third Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA third quarter sales from continuing operations decreased 4.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to
$32.6&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 2.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Sales growth at Walgreens and in the International segment, and sales contributions from the Walgreens Health segment were more than offset by a 720 basis point impact
from the sales decline at AllianceRx Walgreens. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third quarter operating loss from continuing operations was $320&nbsp;million compared to operating
income of $1.1&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating loss in the quarter reflects a $683&nbsp;million charge related to the opioid settlement with the State of Florida and higher costs related to the
Transformational Cost Management Program. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations was $1.0&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 33.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The decline in both adjusted and operating income reflects a decrease
in U.S. pharmacy operating result as it lapped prior year peak <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations, and growth investments in Walgreens Health, partly offset by improved retail contributions in both the U.S. and
International segments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net earnings from continuing operations decreased 73.8&nbsp;percent to $289&nbsp;million compared to $1.1&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. The decline reflects the opioid settlement with the State of Florida, a decrease in U.S. pharmacy operating results as it lapped prior year peak <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
vaccinations, and growth investments in Walgreens Health, partly offset by a gain on the partial sale of the company&#146;s equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen and the favorable impact of a lower tax rate compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, as well as improved retail contributions in both the U.S. and International segments. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations decreased 30.2&nbsp;percent to $834&nbsp;million, down
29.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">EPS from continuing operations
decreased 73.8&nbsp;percent to $0.33 compared to EPS of $1.27 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $0.96, a decrease of 30.0&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and a decrease of
28.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.6&nbsp;billion in the third quarter and free cash flow was
$1.3&nbsp;billion, a $187&nbsp;million decrease in free cash flow compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter driven primarily by lower U.S. operating income, reduced volume from the AllianceRx Walgreens business, and
increased capital expenditures in growth initiatives, partly offset by working capital. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2022 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales from continuing operations in the first nine months of fiscal 2022 were
$100.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of 2.0&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago, and an increase of 2.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting comparable sales growth at Walgreens and in the International segment and
contributions from Walgreens Health acquisitions, partly offset by a decline in sales at AllianceRx Walgreens. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income from continuing
operations in the first nine months of fiscal 2022 increased 54.3&nbsp;percent to $2.2&nbsp;billion compared to $1.4&nbsp;billion in the same period a year ago. This reflects a $1.5&nbsp;billion charge to the company&#146;s equity earnings from
AmerisourceBergen in the prior fiscal year, partly offset by a $683&nbsp;million charge related to the opioid settlement with the State of Florida in the current quarter. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations in the first nine months
of the fiscal year was $4.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of 13.1&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago on a reported basis, and up 13.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increase reflects adjusted gross profit growth across both
pharmacy and retail in the United States and a continued rebound in International segment sales and profitability, partly offset by growth investments in Walgreens Health. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">2
</FONT></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the first nine months of fiscal 2022, net earnings from continuing operations increased $3.1&nbsp;billion compared
to the same period a year earlier, to $4.8&nbsp;billion, reflecting a $2.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain in the first quarter due to the remeasurement of the company&#146;s previously held investments in
VillageMD and Shields, and a $1.2&nbsp;billion charge, net of tax, in the prior fiscal year from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. This was partly offset by the charge related to the Florida opioid settlement in the current
quarter. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations increased 13.3% to $3.7&nbsp;billion, up 13.9% on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS from continuing
operations for the first nine months of fiscal 2022 increased $3.60 to $5.49, compared to the same period a year ago. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $4.23, an increase of 13.3&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago on a reported
basis and an increase of 13.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $3.8&nbsp;billion in the first nine months
of fiscal 2022, a decrease of $497&nbsp;million from the same period last year, and free cash flow was $2.6&nbsp;billion, a decrease of $737&nbsp;million from the same period a year ago driven by reduced volume from the AllianceRx Walgreens
business, the absence of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related government support, and increased capital expenditures in growth initiatives, including the VillageMD footprint expansion and the rollout of new automated
microfulfillment centers, partly offset by working capital initiatives and timing benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Highlights </B></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Building a high-performance culture and winning team </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="11%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Appointed three executives to Walgreens retail products and customer leadership team: Linh Peters as SVP and Chief
Marketing Officer, Luke Rauch as SVP and Chief Merchandising Officer, and Bala Visalatha as SVP and Chief Product Officer </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Introduced Be Well Connected, the company&#146;s team member program for mental health and wellbeing </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Improved the company&#146;s global engagement score to 72, an increase of 2 points from the September 2021 level
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Celebrated Red Nose Day for the eighth consecutive year as the exclusive retailer of the nationwide campaign to help end
the cycle of child poverty and ensure a healthy future for all children </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="21%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#150;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Red Nose Day has raised $275&nbsp;million since launching in the U.S. in 2015, positively impacting the lives of
30&nbsp;million children, and Walgreens has raised more than $140&nbsp;million toward that total </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>United States: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The United States segment had third quarter sales of
$26.7&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 7.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, driven by a decline in the AllianceRx Walgreens business. Comparable sales increased 1.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales decreased 9.7&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, negatively impacted by an 11 percentage point headwind from the AllianceRx Walgreens business. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 2.0&nbsp;percent in the quarter compared to a year ago. Comparable prescriptions filled decreased
1.8&nbsp;percent; excluding immunizations, comparable prescriptions increased 2.1&nbsp;percent. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter decreased 2.5&nbsp;percent to 304&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales increased 1.0&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales increased 1.4&nbsp;percent compared to
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> comparable retail sales increased 2.4&nbsp;percent. The increase reflects strong growth in health and wellness,
which increased 7.9&nbsp;percent aided by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">at-home</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> tests and cough cold flu and a 2.6&nbsp;percent increase in personal care, partly offset by beauty, and
consumables and general merchandise, which decreased 0.4&nbsp;percent and 1.9&nbsp;percent, respectively. Consumables and general merchandise lapped strong sales in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related items and were impacted by
the planned decline in tobacco. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 9.8&nbsp;percent to $5.5&nbsp;billion compared to $6.1&nbsp;billion in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted gross profit decreased 9.6&nbsp;percent to $5.6&nbsp;billion compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting a decline in pharmacy results as it
lapped prior year peak <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations, partly offset by positive contributions from retail performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selling,
general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) increased 15.0&nbsp;percent to $5.7&nbsp;billion compared to $5.0&nbsp;billion in the year ago quarter, including a $683&nbsp;million charge related to an accrual for the aforementioned opioid
settlement with the State of Florida and higher costs related to the Transformational Cost Management Program. Adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 0.9&nbsp;percent to $4.8&nbsp;billion, driven by lower volumes of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and cost discipline, partly offset by increased labor costs and the timing of marketing expenditures. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">4 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss in the third quarter decreased to $90&nbsp;million compared to operating income of $1.2&nbsp;billion in
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting the opioid settlement with the State of Florida and higher Transformational Cost Management Program costs. Adjusted operating income decreased 34.4&nbsp;percent to
$966&nbsp;million compared to $1.5&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting strong prior period results which included peak <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccination volumes, with
positive contributions from growth at retail in the current period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The International segment had third quarter sales of $5.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of 0.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 9.0&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 9.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, with Boots UK sales growing 13.5&nbsp;percent, and our German wholesale business growing 6.8&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales decreased 0.4&nbsp;percent<STRIKE> </STRIKE>compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Growth in
comparable National Health Service (NHS) volumes was more than offset by favorable timing on NHS reimbursement in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 24.0&nbsp;percent compared to
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, with market share gains across all categories, led by beauty. Footfall improved compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; however, traffic remains below <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID-19</FONT></FONT> levels. Boots.com continued to perform well, accounting for over 13&nbsp;percent of retail sales in the quarter compared to 6&nbsp;percent <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased 3.2&nbsp;percent compared to the same quarter a year ago, including an adverse currency
impact of 8.0&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross profit increased 11.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong sales growth in the UK. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in
the quarter decreased 2.9&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $1.0&nbsp;billion, including a favorable currency impact of 7.0&nbsp;percent. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased 2.4&nbsp;percent on a constant
currency basis. Excluding currency impacts, the increase in both SG&amp;A and adjusted SG&amp;A reflects increased investments in labor and marketing, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related government support in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, partly offset by a gain in the UK from a leaseback transaction. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income increased to $100&nbsp;million
compared to $36&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating income was negatively impacted 36.9 percentage points ($13&nbsp;million) as a result of currency translation. Adjusted operating income grew
strongly to $174&nbsp;million, more than doubling the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Walgreens Health:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company&#146;s Walgreens Health segment, created at the beginning of fiscal year 2022, is a consumer-centric, technology-enabled healthcare business that
engages consumers through a personalized, omnichannel experience across the care journey. Walgreens Health will deliver improved health outcomes and lower costs for payors and providers by delivering care through owned and partnered assets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Walgreens Health segment currently consists of: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">A majority position in VillageMD, a leading, national provider of value-based primary care services; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">A majority position in Shields, a specialty pharmacy integrator and accelerator for hospitals; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The Walgreens Health organically-developed business that contracts with payors and providers to deliver clinical healthcare
services to their members and members&#146; caregivers through both digital and physical channels. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Walgreens Health segment had third quarter
sales of $596&nbsp;million. On a pro forma basis, compared to their <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> standalone results, these businesses grew sales at a combined rate of 65&nbsp;percent in the quarter. Shields grew 47&nbsp;percent,
driven by key contract wins, further expansion of existing partnerships, and strong executional focus. VillageMD grew 69&nbsp;percent, reflecting existing clinic growth and footprint expansion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">5 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross loss and adjusted gross loss were each $21&nbsp;million. Shields gross profit, driven by further growth at
existing partnerships and expanding margins, was more than offset by growth investments at VillageMD. As of the end of the third quarter, VillageMD had 315 total clinics open, an increase of 97 clinics compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Third quarter SG&amp;A was $213&nbsp;million, and adjusted SG&amp;A was $108&nbsp;million reflecting the
two acquisitions, as well as continued investments in the Walgreens Health organically-developed business. Adjusted SG&amp;A excludes certain costs related to stock compensation expense and amortization of acquired intangible assets. Operating loss
was $234&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating loss was $129&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will hold a conference call to discuss the third quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, 2022. The conference call will be simulcast through the
WBA investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A replay of the conference call will be archived on the website for 12 months after the call. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">7 </FONT></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an
integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 13,000 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. The company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health
services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA has more than 315,000 team members and a presence in nine countries through its portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty Company,
Benavides in Mexico and Ahumada in Chile. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been recognized for
its commitment to operating sustainably: it is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI) and was named to the 100 Best Corporate Citizens 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:80pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(WBA-ER)</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented
in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These
supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency
translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute
for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company does not provide
a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available
without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact
diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company also presents certain information related to
current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange
rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this
presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the company&#146;s United States and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least 12
consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months as well as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for
the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable
retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same
as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented
on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>

prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">14 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings, including legal defense costs. During the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2022, the Company recorded a $683&nbsp;million charge related to a settlement agreement with the State of Florida to resolve all claims related to the
distribution and dispensing of prescription opioid medications across the Company&#146;s pharmacies in the State of Florida. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a
predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks and contract intangibles.
Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated
intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset
becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to measure acquired
inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments excludes the expected profit margin component from cost
of sales recorded under the business combination accounting principles. Stock based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair
valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from
acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen&#146;s recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its
financial statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include charges incurred related to certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in operating income, for example, costs related to integration efforts for successful merger,
acquisition and divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance and stock compensation. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by
the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s United States segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the United States segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be
impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of equity method investment and investment in equity securities includes impairment of certain investments. The
Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business and it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis. Exclusion of such charges enables more
consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Other income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended February&nbsp;28, 2022, the Company finalized the working capital adjustments with
AmerisourceBergen related to the sale of the Alliance Healthcare business, resulting in a $38&nbsp;million charge recorded to Other income in the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within Other income. We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying derivative
instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on the sale of equity method investments. During the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2022, the
Company recorded a gain of $424&nbsp;million in Other income due to a partial sale of its equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen. During the three months and nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021, the Company recorded gains of $98&nbsp;million
and $290&nbsp;million, respectively, in Other income due to a partial sale of its equity method investment in Option Care Health. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">11</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on business combinations due to the remeasurement of previously held minority equity interests
and debt securities to fair value. During the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2021, the Company recorded such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gains of $2.2&nbsp;billion and $402&nbsp;million for VillageMD and Shields,
respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2022, the Company incurred a $4&nbsp;million loss in connection with the early
extinguishment of debt related to the integration of Shields. In the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021, the Company incurred a $419&nbsp;million loss related to the Company&#146;s cash tender offers to partially purchase and retire
$3.3&nbsp;billion of long-term U.S. denominated notes. The Company excludes these charges as related activities do not reflect the Company&#146;s ongoing financial performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision (benefit) include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision (benefit) commensurate
with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income tax
provision (benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share of certain equity
method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded within post tax
earnings from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments
are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect
all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. In the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021, due to partial sales of ownership interests in Option Care Health, our then equity method investee HC Group Holdings lost the ability to control
Option Care Health and, therefore, deconsolidated Option Care Health in its financial statements. As a result of this deconsolidation, HC Group Holdings recognized a gain of $1.2&nbsp;billion and the Company recorded its share of equity earnings in
HC Group Holdings of $576&nbsp;million during the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-month</FONT> reporting lag, operating (loss) income for the three and nine month period ended May&nbsp;31, 2022 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period of January&nbsp;1, 2022 through
March&nbsp;31, 2022 and the period of July&nbsp;1, 2021 through March&nbsp;31, 2022, respectively. Operating (loss) income for the three and nine month period ended May&nbsp;31, 2021 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period
of January&nbsp;1, 2021 through March&nbsp;31, 2021 and the period of July&nbsp;1, 2020 through March&nbsp;31, 2021, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

AmerisourceBergen and adjusted equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL">NM&#151;Not meaningful. Percentage increases above 200% or when one period includes income and other period includes loss are considered
not meaningful. </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
